## 项目架构（当前）
- 可运行目录：`./`（仓库根目录）
- 可维护层：`architecture/`
- 启动编排层：`architecture/boot/`
- 规范文档层：`architecture/docs/`

## 入口与启动链路
1. 入口文件：`game.js`
2. 桥接入口：`architecture/boot/game-bootstrap.js`
3. 启动主流程：`bootGameRuntime -> runBootSequence -> startApplicationLifecycle`
4. 关键启动模块：
- `architecture/boot/app-lifecycle.js`
- `architecture/boot/boot-logger.js`
- `architecture/boot/config.js`
- `architecture/boot/game-bootstrap.js`
- `architecture/boot/global-context.js`
- `architecture/boot/render-policies.js`
- `architecture/boot/runtime-bridge.js`
- `architecture/boot/system-info.js`
